\doxysubsection{详细描述}
class to create an executor for running a taskflow graph 

class to create an executor

An executor manages a set of worker threads to run one or multiple taskflows using an efficient work-\/stealing scheduling algorithm.

\end{DoxyCode}


All the {\ttfamily run} methods are {\itshape thread-\/safe}. You can submit multiple taskflows at the same time to an executor from different threads.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Executor()}{Executor()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/5]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classtf_1_1_executor_a4910e89d89146b6d563d598b795eb4a9} 
tf\+::\+Executor\+::\+Executor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{N}{ = {\ttfamily std\+:\+:thread\+:\+:hardware\+\_\+concurrency()}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [explicit]}}



constructs the executor with {\ttfamily N} worker threads 


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em N} & the number of workers (default std\+::thread\+::hardware\+\_\+concurrency)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The constructor spawns {\ttfamily N} worker threads to run tasks in a work-\/stealing loop. The number of workers must be greater than zero or an exception will be thrown. By default, the number of worker threads is equal to the maximum hardware concurrency returned by std\+::thread\+::hardware\+\_\+concurrency. 函数调用图\+:

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Executor()}{Executor()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [5/5]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classtf_1_1_executor_a23b4c858279616d79612dccd9a715365} 
tf\+::\+Executor\+::\+Executor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{N}{ = {\ttfamily std\+:\+:thread\+:\+:hardware\+\_\+concurrency()}, }\item[{std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_worker_interface}{Worker\+Interface}} $>$}]{wix}{ = {\ttfamily nullptr}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [explicit]}}



constructs the executor with {\ttfamily N} worker threads 


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em N} & number of workers (default std\+::thread\+::hardware\+\_\+concurrency) \\
\hline
{\em wix} & interface class instance to configure workers\textquotesingle{} behaviors\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The constructor spawns {\ttfamily N} worker threads to run tasks in a work-\/stealing loop. The number of workers must be greater than zero or an exception will be thrown. By default, the number of worker threads is equal to the maximum hardware concurrency returned by std\+::thread\+::hardware\+\_\+concurrency.

Users can alter the worker behavior, such as changing thread affinity, via deriving an instance from \doxylink{classtf_1_1_worker_interface}{tf\+::\+Worker\+Interface}. 函数调用图\+:
% FIG 3

destructs the executor

\Hypertarget{classtf_1_1_executor_a1e6866c8f1b6a2e932f06d0b4eb032c0}\index{tf::Executor@{tf::Executor}!async@{async}}
\index{async@{async}!tf::Executor@{tf::Executor}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{async()}{async()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/9]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classtf_1_1_executor_a1e6866c8f1b6a2e932f06d0b4eb032c0} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{test__flow__graph_8cpp_a1c83625ec20fd09ecaf0e5b37c75f6f8}{F}}, typename... ArgsT$>$ \\
auto tf\+::\+Executor\+::async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{test__flow__graph_8cpp_a1c83625ec20fd09ecaf0e5b37c75f6f8}{F}} \&\&}]{f}{, }\item[{ArgsT \&\&...}]{args}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



runs a given function asynchronously 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em F} & callable type \\
\hline
{\em ArgsT} & parameter types\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em f} & callable object to call \\
\hline
{\em args} & parameters to pass to the callable\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future} that will holds the result of the execution
\end{DoxyReturn}
The method creates an asynchronous task to launch the given function on the given arguments. Unlike std\+::async, the return here is a {\itshape \doxylink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future}} that holds an optional object to the result. If the asynchronous task is cancelled before it runs, the return is a {\ttfamily std\+::nullopt}, or the value returned by the callable.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{tf::Future<std::optional<int>>\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceluisa_1_1fiber_ade0f9c58b88c65b0e9c7be95852327ff}{future}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{thread__pool_8cpp_a543e564a8407bbeac15cb2d929fec755}{executor}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_executor_af960048056f7c6b5bc71f4f526f05df7}{async}}([]()\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ std::cout\ <<\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}create\ an\ asynchronous\ task\ and\ returns\ 1\(\backslash\)n"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}

\end{DoxyCode}


This member function is thread-\/safe. 函数调用图\+:

\index{corun@{corun}!tf::Executor@{tf::Executor}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{corun()}{corun()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classtf_1_1_executor_a8fcd9e0557922bb8194999f0cd433ea8} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::\+Executor\+::corun (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}} \&}]{target}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



runs a target graph and waits until it completes using an internal worker of this executor 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em T} & target type which has {\ttfamily \doxylink{classtf_1_1_graph}{tf\+::\+Graph}\& T\+::graph()} defined \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em target} & the target task graph object\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The method runs a target graph which has {\ttfamily \doxylink{classtf_1_1_graph}{tf\+::\+Graph}\& T\+::graph()} defined and waits until the execution completes. Unlike the typical flow of calling {\ttfamily \doxylink{classtf_1_1_executor_a519777f5783981d534e9e53b99712069}{tf\+::\+Executor\+::run}} series plus waiting on the result, this method must be called by an internal worker of this executor. The caller worker will participate in the work-\/stealing loop of the scheduler, thereby avoiding potential deadlock caused by blocked waiting.

\end{DoxyCode}


The method is thread-\/safe as long as the target is not concurrently ran by two or more threads.

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
You must call \doxylink{classtf_1_1_executor_a8fcd9e0557922bb8194999f0cd433ea8}{tf\+::\+Executor\+::corun} from a worker of the calling executor or an exception will be thrown. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

runs a target graph and waits until it completes using an internal worker of this executor 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em T} & target type which has {\ttfamily \doxylink{classtf_1_1_graph}{tf\+::\+Graph}\& T\+::graph()} defined \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em target} & the target task graph object\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The method runs a target graph which has {\ttfamily \doxylink{classtf_1_1_graph}{tf\+::\+Graph}\& T\+::graph()} defined and waits until the execution completes. Unlike the typical flow of calling {\ttfamily \doxylink{classtf_1_1_executor_a519777f5783981d534e9e53b99712069}{tf\+::\+Executor\+::run}} series plus waiting on the result, this method must be called by an internal worker of this executor. The caller worker will participate in the work-\/stealing loop of the scheduler, thereby avoiding potential deadlock caused by blocked waiting.

The method is thread-\/safe as long as the target is not concurrently ran by two or more threads.

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
You must call \doxylink{classtf_1_1_executor_a8fcd9e0557922bb8194999f0cd433ea8}{tf\+::\+Executor\+::corun} from a worker of the calling executor or an exception will be thrown. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{test__flow__graph_8cpp_a1c83625ec20fd09ecaf0e5b37c75f6f8}{F}}, typename I, std\+::enable\+\_\+if\+\_\+t$<$!std\+::is\+\_\+same\+\_\+v$<$ std\+::decay\+\_\+t$<$ I $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_async_task}{Async\+Task}} $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} $>$ \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}$>$ \\
auto tf\+::\+Executor\+::dependent\+\_\+async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{test__flow__graph_8cpp_a1c83625ec20fd09ecaf0e5b37c75f6f8}{F}} \&\&}]{func}{, }\item[{I}]{first}{, }\item[{I}]{last}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



runs the given function asynchronously when the given range of dependents finish 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em F} & callable type \\
\hline
{\em I} & iterator type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em func} & callable object \\
\hline
{\em first} & iterator to the beginning (inclusive) \\
\hline
{\em last} & iterator to the end (exclusive)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a pair of a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_async_task}{tf\+::\+Async\+Task} handle and a @std\+\_\+future that holds the result of the execution
\end{DoxyReturn}
The example below creates three asynchronous tasks, {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}, and {\ttfamily C}, in which task {\ttfamily C} runs after task {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}} and task {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}. \doxylink{classtf_1_1_task}{Task} {\ttfamily C} returns a pair of its \doxylink{classtf_1_1_async_task}{tf\+::\+Async\+Task} handle and a std\+::future$<$int$>$ that eventually will hold the result of the execution.

template$<$typename Observer, typename... ArgsT$>$ \\

constructs an observer to inspect the activities of worker threads 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em Observer} & observer type derived from \doxylink{classtf_1_1_observer_interface}{tf\+::\+Observer\+Interface} \\
\hline
{\em ArgsT} & argument parameter pack\\

\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em args} & arguments to forward to the constructor of the observer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a shared pointer to the created observer
\end{DoxyReturn}
Each executor manages a list of observers with shared ownership with callers. For each of these observers, the two member functions, \doxylink{classtf_1_1_observer_interface_a8225fcacb03089677a1efc4b16b734cc}{tf\+::\+Observer\+Interface\+::on\+\_\+entry} and \doxylink{classtf_1_1_observer_interface_aa22f5378154653f08d9a58326bda4754}{tf\+::\+Observer\+Interface\+::on\+\_\+exit} will be called before and after the execution of a task.

This member function is not thread-\/safe. \Hypertarget{classtf_1_1_executor_aff77def96ae740d648dd84e571237c83}\index{tf::Executor@{tf::Executor}!make\_observer@{make\_observer}}

\index{make\_observer@{make\_observer}!tf::Executor@{tf::Executor}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{make\_observer()}{make\_observer()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/5]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classtf_1_1_executor_aff77def96ae740d648dd84e571237c83} 
template$<$typename Observer, typename... ArgsT$>$ \\
std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr$<$ Observer $>$ tf\+::\+Executor\+::make\+\_\+observer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{ArgsT \&\&...}]{args}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



constructs an observer to inspect the activities of worker threads 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em Observer} & observer type derived from \doxylink{classtf_1_1_observer_interface}{tf\+::\+Observer\+Interface} \\
\hline
{\em ArgsT} & argument parameter pack\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em args} & arguments to forward to the constructor of the observer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a shared pointer to the created observer
\end{DoxyReturn}
Each executor manages a list of observers with shared ownership with callers. For each of these observers, the two member functions, \doxylink{classtf_1_1_observer_interface_a8225fcacb03089677a1efc4b16b734cc}{tf\+::\+Observer\+Interface\+::on\+\_\+entry} and \doxylink{classtf_1_1_observer_interface_aa22f5378154653f08d9a58326bda4754}{tf\+::\+Observer\+Interface\+::on\+\_\+exit} will be called before and after the execution of a task.

This member function is not thread-\/safe. 函数调用图\+:

For each of these observers, the two member functions, \doxylink{classtf_1_1_observer_interface_a8225fcacb03089677a1efc4b16b734cc}{tf\+::\+Observer\+Interface\+::on\+\_\+entry} and \doxylink{classtf_1_1_observer_interface_aa22f5378154653f08d9a58326bda4754}{tf\+::\+Observer\+Interface\+::on\+\_\+exit} will be called before and after the execution of a task.

\Hypertarget{classtf_1_1_executor_a51acee1670e9f246c7ccd7f6a63f1524}\index{tf::Executor@{tf::Executor}!named\_async@{named\_async}}
\index{named\_async@{named\_async}!tf::Executor@{tf::Executor}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{named\_async()}{named\_async()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classtf_1_1_executor_a51acee1670e9f246c7ccd7f6a63f1524} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{test__flow__graph_8cpp_a1c83625ec20fd09ecaf0e5b37c75f6f8}{F}}, typename... ArgsT$>$ \\
auto tf\+::\+Executor\+::named\+\_\+async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::string \&}]{name}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{test__flow__graph_8cpp_a1c83625ec20fd09ecaf0e5b37c75f6f8}{F}} \&\&}]{f}{, }\item[{ArgsT \&\&...}]{args}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



runs a given function asynchronously and gives a name to this task 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em F} & callable type \\
\hline
{\em ArgsT} & parameter types\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em name} & name of the asynchronous task \\
\hline
{\em f} & callable object to call \\
\hline
{\em args} & parameters to pass to the callable\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future} that will holds the result of the execution
\end{DoxyReturn}
The method creates a named asynchronous task to launch the given function on the given arguments. Naming an asynchronous task is primarily used for profiling and visualizing the task execution timeline. Unlike std\+::async, the return here is a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future} that holds an optional object to the result. If the asynchronous task is cancelled before it runs, the return is a {\ttfamily std\+::nullopt}, or the value returned by the callable.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{tf::Future<std::optional<int>>\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceluisa_1_1fiber_ade0f9c58b88c65b0e9c7be95852327ff}{future}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{thread__pool_8cpp_a543e564a8407bbeac15cb2d929fec755}{executor}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_executor_a51acee1670e9f246c7ccd7f6a63f1524}{named\_async}}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}name"{}},\ []()\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ std::cout\ <<\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}create\ an\ asynchronous\ task\ with\ a\ name\ and\ returns\ 1\(\backslash\)n"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}

\end{DoxyCode}


This member function is thread-\/safe. 函数调用图\+:

similar to \doxylink{classtf_1_1_executor_a51acee1670e9f246c7ccd7f6a63f1524}{tf\+::\+Executor\+::named\+\_\+async} but does not return a future object

\Hypertarget{classtf_1_1_executor_a6d6c28ed58211e4c27a99571e5bf0b6c}\index{tf::Executor@{tf::Executor}!num\_topologies@{num\_topologies}}
\index{num\_topologies@{num\_topologies}!tf::Executor@{tf::Executor}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{num\_topologies()}{num\_topologies()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/5]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classtf_1_1_executor_a6d6c28ed58211e4c27a99571e5bf0b6c} 
size\+\_\+t tf\+::\+Executor\+::num\+\_\+topologies (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



queries the number of running topologies at the time of this call 

When a taskflow is submitted to an executor, a topology is created to store runtime metadata of the running taskflow. When the execution of the submitted taskflow finishes, its corresponding topology will be removed from the executor.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{num\_topologies()}{num\_topologies()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/5]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classtf_1_1_executor_a6d6c28ed58211e4c27a99571e5bf0b6c} 
size\+\_\+t tf\+::\+Executor\+::num\+\_\+topologies (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



queries the number of running topologies at the time of this call 

When a taskflow is submitted to an executor, a topology is created to store runtime metadata of the running taskflow. When the execution of the submitted taskflow finishes, its corresponding topology will be removed from the executor.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{thread__pool_8cpp_a543e564a8407bbeac15cb2d929fec755}{executor}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_executor_a519777f5783981d534e9e53b99712069}{run}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{poisson_8hpp_aa56fe360bb0ae38e0082f49e394ff825}{taskflow}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{std::cout\ <<\ \mbox{\hyperlink{thread__pool_8cpp_a543e564a8407bbeac15cb2d929fec755}{executor}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_executor_a6d6c28ed58211e4c27a99571e5bf0b6c}{num\_topologies}}();\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 0\ or\ 1\ (taskflow\ still\ running)}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} $>$ tf\+::\+Executor\+::run (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_taskflow}{Taskflow}} \&\&}]{taskflow}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



runs a moved taskflow once 


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em taskflow} & a moved \doxylink{classtf_1_1_taskflow}{tf\+::\+Taskflow} object\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future} that holds the result of the execution
\end{DoxyReturn}
This member function executes a moved taskflow once and returns a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future} object that eventually holds the result of the execution. The executor will take care of the lifetime of the moved taskflow.

\end{DoxyParams}

This member function is thread-\/safe.

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} $>$ tf\+::\+Executor\+::run\+\_\+n (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_taskflow}{Taskflow}} \&\&}]{taskflow}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{N}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



runs a moved taskflow for {\ttfamily N} times 


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em taskflow} & a moved \doxylink{classtf_1_1_taskflow}{tf\+::\+Taskflow} object \\
\hline
{\em N} & number of runs\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future} that holds the result of the execution
\end{DoxyReturn}
This member function executes a moved taskflow {\ttfamily N} times and returns a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future} object that eventually holds the result of the execution. The executor will take care of the lifetime of the moved taskflow.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} $>$ tf\+::\+Executor\+::run\+\_\+n (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_taskflow}{Taskflow}} \&\&}]{taskflow}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{N}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



runs a moved taskflow for {\ttfamily N} times 


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em taskflow} & a moved \doxylink{classtf_1_1_taskflow}{tf\+::\+Taskflow} object \\
\hline
{\em N} & number of runs\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future} that holds the result of the execution
\end{DoxyReturn}
This member function executes a moved taskflow {\ttfamily N} times and returns a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future} object that eventually holds the result of the execution. The executor will take care of the lifetime of the moved taskflow.

This member function is thread-\/safe.

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
The executor does not own the given taskflow. It is your responsibility to ensure the taskflow remains alive during its execution. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} $>$ tf\+::\+Executor\+::run\+\_\+until (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_taskflow}{Taskflow}} \&\&}]{taskflow}{, }\item[{P \&\&}]{pred}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_aaee470c3acb6b181fd804d072284fbaa}{C}} \&\&}]{callable}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



runs a moved taskflow and keeps running it until the predicate becomes true and then invokes the callback 


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em taskflow} & a moved \doxylink{classtf_1_1_taskflow}{tf\+::\+Taskflow} \\
\hline
{\em pred} & a boolean predicate to return {\ttfamily true} for stop \\
\hline
{\em callable} & a callable object to be invoked after this run completes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future} that holds the result of the execution
\end{DoxyReturn}
This member function executes a moved taskflow multiple times until the predicate returns {\ttfamily true} and then invokes the given callable when the execution completes. This member function returns a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_future}{tf\+::\+Future} object that eventually holds the result of the execution. The executor will take care of the lifetime of the moved taskflow.

{\em func} & callable object\\

The method creates an asynchronous task to run the given function without returning any @std\+\_\+future object. This member function is more efficient than \doxylink{classtf_1_1_executor_af960048056f7c6b5bc71f4f526f05df7}{tf\+::\+Executor\+::async} and is encouraged to use when applications do not need a @std\+\_\+future to acquire the result or synchronize the execution.

{\em func} & callable object\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The method creates an asynchronous task to run the given function without returning any @std\+\_\+future object. This member function is more efficient than \doxylink{classtf_1_1_executor_af960048056f7c6b5bc71f4f526f05df7}{tf\+::\+Executor\+::async} and is encouraged to use when applications do not need a @std\+\_\+future to acquire the result or synchronize the execution.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_async_task}{tf\+::\+Async\+Task} handle
\end{DoxyReturn}
This member function is more efficient than \doxylink{classtf_1_1_executor_aee02b63d3a91ad5ca5a1c0e71f3e128f}{tf\+::\+Executor\+::dependent\+\_\+async} and is encouraged to use when you do not want a @std\+\_\+future to acquire the result or synchronize the execution. The example below creates three asynchronous tasks, {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}, and {\ttfamily C}, in which task {\ttfamily C} runs after task {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}} and task {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_async_task}{tf\+::\+Async\+Task}} tf\+::\+Executor\+::silent\+\_\+dependent\+\_\+async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{test__flow__graph_8cpp_a1c83625ec20fd09ecaf0e5b37c75f6f8}{F}} \&\&}]{func}{, }\item[{I}]{first}{, }\item[{I}]{last}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\end{DoxyReturn}
This member function is more efficient than \doxylink{classtf_1_1_executor_aee02b63d3a91ad5ca5a1c0e71f3e128f}{tf\+::\+Executor\+::dependent\+\_\+async} and is encouraged to use when you do not want a @std\+\_\+future to acquire the result or synchronize the execution. The example below creates three asynchronous tasks, {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}, and {\ttfamily C}, in which task {\ttfamily C} runs after task {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}} and task {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}.

runs the given function asynchronously when the given predecessors finish

This member function is more efficient than \doxylink{classtf_1_1_executor_aee02b63d3a91ad5ca5a1c0e71f3e128f}{tf\+::\+Executor\+::dependent\+\_\+async} and is encouraged to use when you do not want a @std\+\_\+future to acquire the result or synchronize the execution. The example below creates three asynchronous tasks, {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}, and {\ttfamily C}, in which task {\ttfamily C} runs after task {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}} and task {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_async_task}{tf\+::\+Async\+Task}} tf\+::\+Executor\+::silent\+\_\+dependent\+\_\+async (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{P \&\&}]{params}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{test__flow__graph_8cpp_a1c83625ec20fd09ecaf0e5b37c75f6f8}{F}} \&\&}]{func}{, }\item[{I}]{first}{, }\item[{I}]{last}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



runs the given function asynchronously when the given range of predecessors finish

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}

\end{DoxyReturn}
This member function is more efficient than \doxylink{classtf_1_1_executor_aee02b63d3a91ad5ca5a1c0e71f3e128f}{tf\+::\+Executor\+::dependent\+\_\+async} and is encouraged to use when you do not want a @std\+\_\+future to acquire the result or synchronize the execution. The example below creates three asynchronous tasks, {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}, and {\ttfamily C}, in which task {\ttfamily C} runs after task {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}} and task {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}. Assigned task names will appear in the observers of the executor.

runs the given function asynchronously when the given predecessors finish 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em F} & callable type \\
\hline
{\em Tasks} & task types convertible to \doxylink{classtf_1_1_async_task}{tf\+::\+Async\+Task}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em params} & task parameters \\
\hline
{\em func} & callable object \\
\hline
{\em tasks} & asynchronous tasks on which this execution depends\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a \doxylink{classtf_1_1_async_task}{tf\+::\+Async\+Task} handle
\end{DoxyReturn}
This member function is more efficient than \doxylink{classtf_1_1_executor_aee02b63d3a91ad5ca5a1c0e71f3e128f}{tf\+::\+Executor\+::dependent\+\_\+async} and is encouraged to use when you do not want a @std\+\_\+future to acquire the result or synchronize the execution. The example below creates three asynchronous tasks, {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}, and {\ttfamily C}, in which task {\ttfamily C} runs after task {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}} and task {\ttfamily \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}. Assigned task names will appear in the observers of the executor.

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_ae4f82344f573c70aa1066a2394bba345}{int}} tf\+::\+Executor\+::this\+\_\+worker\+\_\+id (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



queries the id of the caller thread in this executor 

Each worker has an unique id in the range of {\ttfamily 0} to {\ttfamily N-\/1} associated with its parent executor. If the caller thread does not belong to the executor, {\ttfamily -\/1} is returned.

\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::\+Executor\+::wait\+\_\+for\+\_\+all (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



waits for all tasks to complete 

This member function waits until all submitted tasks (e.\+g., taskflows, asynchronous tasks) to finish.
